#MESSAGE CC013C
##Properties
<table class="table width-min-100">

   CC013C
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td class="label">
   Name
  </td>
  <td>
   Declaration Amendment
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr>
  <td class="label">
   Description
  </td>
  <td>

  </td>
 </tr>
